✅ 4. Write a Minimal React UI That Talks to Backend
Example: Query Genes of Interest (Knowledge API)
Create a page:
frontend/src/pages/GeneFinder.jsx

import { useState } from "react";
import { API_BASE } from "../config";

export default function GeneFinder() {
  const [phenotype, setPhenotype] = useState("");
  const [results, setResults] = useState(null);

  const search = async () => {
    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/knowledge/${phenotype}`);
    const data = await res.json();
    setResults(data);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Find Genes Associated With a Phenotype</h2>
      <input
        value={phenotype}
        onChange={(e) => setPhenotype(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="e.g. root color"
      />
      <button onClick={search}>Search</button>

      {results && (
        <pre>{JSON.stringify(results, null, 2)}</pre>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
✅ 5. Example Page: Run Similarity Search
frontend/src/pages/Similarity.jsx:

import { useState } from "react";
import { API_BASE } from "../config";

export default function Similarity() {
  const [genes, setGenes] = useState("");
  const [reference, setReference] = useState("");
  const [response, setResponse] = useState(null);

  const run = async () => {
    const req = {
      phenotype_blocks: [{ genes: genes.split(",") }],
      reference_accession: reference,
      similarity_measure: "numeric"
    };

    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/similarity`, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(req)
    });

    setResponse(await res.json());
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Similarity Search</h2>

      <input
        placeholder="Genes (comma-separated)"
        value={genes}
        onChange={(e) => setGenes(e.target.value)}
      />

      <input
        placeholder="Reference Accession"
        value={reference}
        onChange={(e) => setReference(e.target.value)}
      />

      <button onClick={run}>Compute</button>

      {response && (
        <pre>{JSON.stringify(response, null, 2)}</pre>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
✅ 6. Add Routes to Your App
src/App.jsx:

import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from "react-router-dom";
import Home from "./pages/Home";
import GeneFinder from "./pages/GeneFinder";
import Similarity from "./pages/Similarity";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/" element={<Home />} />
        <Route path="/genes" element={<GeneFinder />} />
        <Route path="/similarity" element={<Similarity />} />
      </Routes>
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}

You said:
http://localhost:8000/api/association gives {"detail":"Not Found"}
ChatGPT said:
{"detail": "Not Found"} means FastAPI never registered your association router, or it is mounted under a different prefix.

This is easy to fix.

Below is exactly what is happening and how to fix it.

✅ 1. Your Routers Are Defined But Not Mounted
You showed:

backend/api/association.py

backend/api/similarity.py

backend/api/knowledge.py

backend/api/dimensionality.py

Each file defines:

router = APIRouter()
…but you never showed how app.py includes them.

FastAPI won’t automatically discover routers — you must include them manually.

✅ 2. Fix app.py
Edit backend/app.py to look like this:

from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

# Import routers
from backend.api.association import router as association_router
from backend.api.similarity import router as similarity_router
from backend.api.knowledge import router as knowledge_router
from backend.api.dimensionality import router as dimensionality_router

app = FastAPI()

# CORS so frontend can connect
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Mount routers
app.include_router(association_router, prefix="/api/association")
app.include_router(similarity_router, prefix="/api/similarity")
app.include_router(knowledge_router, prefix="/api/knowledge")
app.include_router(dimensionality_router, prefix="/api/dimensionality")

✅ 1. Update backend/app.py (copy/paste this)
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

app = FastAPI(title="CRUNCH API", version="1.0.0")

# CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Import routers AFTER app creation
from backend.api.similarity import router as sim_router
from backend.api.association import router as assoc_router
from backend.api.knowledge import router as knowledge_router
from backend.api.visualisation import router as viz_router

# Register routers under /api/ prefix
app.include_router(sim_router, prefix="/api/similarity")
app.include_router(assoc_router, prefix="/api/association")
app.include_router(knowledge_router, prefix="/api/knowledge")
app.include_router(viz_router, prefix="/api/visualisation")

@app.get("/")
def root():
    return {"status": "CRUNCH API running", "version": "1.0.0"}

Create (or update) a file:

frontend/src/api.js

export const API_BASE = "http://localhost:8000/api";

export async function fetchAssociation(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API_BASE}/association/`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

export async function fetchSimilarity(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API_BASE}/similarity/`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

export async function fetchKnowledge(phenotype) {
  return fetch(`${API_BASE}/knowledge/${phenotype}`).then(r => r.json());
}

export async function fetchPcaMds(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API_BASE}/visualisation/pca_mds`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

1) Backend — tiny helper endpoints
Add a new file backend/api/utility.py:

# backend/api/utility.py
from fastapi import APIRouter
from backend.data.load_data import carrot_data

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/data/samples")
def list_samples():
    # return the sample list for UI dropdowns
    return {"samples": carrot_data.samples}

@router.get("/ping")
def ping():
    return {"message": "Backend is alive"}
Then update backend/app.py to include this router (you already updated before, just include utility):

# backend/app.py (add import & include)
from backend.api.utility import router as util_router

# ... existing include_router calls ...

app.include_router(util_router, prefix="/api")
(If you already have app.include_router(... prefix="/api") mapping for other routers, this just puts /api/data/samples and /api/ping alongside them.)

Restart backend:

uvicorn backend.app:app --reload
Verify:

http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/ping → {"message":"Backend is alive"}

http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/data/samples → {"samples":[...names...]}

2) Frontend — API client
Create/replace frontend/src/api.js:

// frontend/src/api.js
export const API_BASE = "http://localhost:8000/api";

async function fetchJson(url, opts = {}) {
  const res = await fetch(url, opts);
  const txt = await res.text();
  try {
    const data = txt ? JSON.parse(txt) : null;
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data?.error ?? txt ?? res.statusText);
    return data;
  } catch (err) {
    if (!res.ok) throw err;
    throw err;
  }
}

export async function pingBackend() {
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/ping`);
}

export async function getSamples() {
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/data/samples`);
}

export async function runSimilarity({ phenotype_blocks, combine = "union", similarity_measure = "numeric", reference_accession }) {
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/similarity/`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ phenotype_blocks, combine, similarity_measure, reference_accession })
  });
}

export async function runPcaMds({ phenotype_blocks, combine = "union" }) {
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/visualisation/pca_mds`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({ phenotype_blocks, combine })
  });
}

export async function searchKnowledge(phenotype) {
  const encoded = encodeURIComponent(phenotype);
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/knowledge/${encoded}`);
}

export async function runHeatmap(payload) {
  return fetchJson(`${API_BASE}/visualisation/heatmap`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
  });
}
3) Frontend — App routing and layout
Replace frontend/src/App.jsx with this clean router and nav:

// frontend/src/App.jsx
import React from "react";
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Link } from "react-router-dom";

import Home from "./pages/Home";
import GeneFinder from "./pages/GeneFinder";
import Analysis from "./pages/Analysis";
import NotFound from "./pages/NotFound";

export default function App() {
  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <div style={{ padding: 12 }}>
        <nav style={{ marginBottom: 12 }}>
          <Link to="/">Home</Link> {" | "}
          <Link to="/genes">Find genes</Link> {" | "}
          <Link to="/analysis">Run analysis</Link>
        </nav>

        <Routes>
          <Route path="/" element={<Home />} />
          <Route path="/genes" element={<GeneFinder />} />
          <Route path="/analysis" element={<Analysis />} />
          <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />
        </Routes>
      </div>
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}

4) Frontend — Home page (with ping)
Replace/create frontend/src/pages/Home.jsx:

// frontend/src/pages/Home.jsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { pingBackend } from "../api";

export default function Home() {
  const [status, setStatus] = useState("checking...");
  useEffect(() => {
    pingBackend().then(d => setStatus(d.message)).catch(() => setStatus("Cannot reach backend"));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 16 }}>
      <h1>CRUNCH — Carrot SNP Explorer</h1>
      <p>Welcome to the SNP analysis platform.</p>
      <p><strong>Backend status:</strong> {status}</p>
      <p>Use <em>Find genes</em> to locate candidate genes from literature/databases. Use <em>Run analysis</em> to compute accession similarity and PCA/MDS plots.</p>
    </div>
  );
}
5) Frontend — Gene Finder page
Create frontend/src/pages/GeneFinder.jsx:

// frontend/src/pages/GeneFinder.jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import { searchKnowledge } from "../api";

export default function GeneFinder() {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [results, setResults] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  async function doSearch() {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await searchKnowledge(query);
      setResults(res);
    } catch (err) {
      setResults({ error: err.message });
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 12 }}>
      <h2>Find genes associated with a phenotype</h2>

      <div>
        <input value={query} onChange={e => setQuery(e.target.value)} placeholder="e.g. root color" style={{ width: 300 }} />
        <button onClick={doSearch} disabled={!query || loading} style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>Search</button>
      </div>

      {loading && <p>Searching…</p>}

      {results && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
          <pre style={{ whiteSpace: "pre-wrap" }}>{JSON.stringify(results, null, 2)}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
6) Frontend — Analysis page (form to run similarity + PCA/MDS)
Create frontend/src/pages/Analysis.jsx (improved & tested):

// frontend/src/pages/Analysis.jsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { getSamples } from "../api";
import { runSimilarity, runPcaMds } from "../api";
import PcaMdsPlot from "../PcaMdsPlot";

function emptyBlock() {
  return { genes: [""] };
}

export default function Analysis() {
  const [samples, setSamples] = useState([]);
  const [blocks, setBlocks] = useState([emptyBlock()]);
  const [reference, setReference] = useState("");
  const [combine, setCombine] = useState("union");
  const [metric, setMetric] = useState("numeric");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [similarityResults, setSimilarityResults] = useState(null);
  const [pcaData, setPcaData] = useState(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    getSamples().then(d => setSamples(d.samples || [])).catch(() => {});
  }, []);

  function updateGene(blockIndex, geneIndex, value) {
    const c = [...blocks];
    c[blockIndex].genes[geneIndex] = value;
    setBlocks(c);
  }
  function addGene(blockIndex) {
    const c = [...blocks]; c[blockIndex].genes.push(""); setBlocks(c);
  }
  function addBlock() { setBlocks([...blocks, emptyBlock()]); }
  function removeBlock(i) { setBlocks(blocks.filter((_, idx) => idx !== i)); }

  async function handleSimilarity(e) {
    e?.preventDefault();
    setError(null); setLoading(true);
    try {
      const phenotype_blocks = blocks.map(b => ({ genes: b.genes.filter(Boolean).map(s => s.trim()) }));
      const res = await runSimilarity({ phenotype_blocks, combine, similarity_measure: metric, reference_accession: reference });
      setSimilarityResults(res);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.message);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }

  async function handlePca(e) {
    e?.preventDefault();
    setError(null); setLoading(true);
    try {
      const phenotype_blocks = blocks.map(b => ({ genes: b.genes.filter(Boolean).map(s => s.trim()) }));
      const res = await runPcaMds({ phenotype_blocks, combine });
      setPcaData(res);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.message);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 12 }}>
      <h2>Run similarity analysis</h2>
      <div style={{ marginBottom: 8 }}>
        <label>Reference accession: </label>
        <select value={reference} onChange={e => setReference(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="">-- choose --</option>
          {samples.map(s => <option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
        </select>
      </div>

      <div style={{ marginBottom: 8 }}>
        <label>Combine blocks:</label>
        <select value={combine} onChange={e => setCombine(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="union">Union</option>
          <option value="intersection">Intersection</option>
        </select>

        <label style={{ marginLeft: 12 }}>Metric:</label>
        <select value={metric} onChange={e => setMetric(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="numeric">Numeric distance</option>
          <option value="match">Exact match similarity</option>
          <option value="euclidean">Euclidean</option>
          <option value="ibs">IBS</option>
        </select>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h4>Phenotype gene blocks</h4>
        {blocks.map((block, bi) => (
          <div key={bi} style={{ border: "1px solid #ddd", padding: 8, marginBottom: 8 }}>
            <strong>Block {bi+1}</strong>
            <button type="button" onClick={() => removeBlock(bi)} style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>Remove</button>
            <div>
              {block.genes.map((g, gi) => (
                <div key={gi} style={{ marginTop: 6 }}>
                  <input
                    placeholder="Gene ID"
                    value={g}
                    onChange={e => updateGene(bi, gi, e.target.value)}
                  />
                </div>
              ))}
              <button type="button" onClick={() => addGene(bi)} style={{ marginTop: 6 }}>+ Add gene</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
        <button onClick={addBlock}>+ Add block</button>
      </div>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
        <button onClick={handleSimilarity} disabled={loading}>Run similarity</button>
        <button onClick={handlePca} disabled={loading} style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>Run PCA/MDS</button>
      </div>

      {loading && <p>Running analysis…</p>}
      {error && <p style={{ color: "red" }}>{error}</p>}

      {similarityResults && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
          <h3>Similarity results (ref: {similarityResults.reference})</h3>
          <p>Variants used: {similarityResults.n_variants}</p>
          <table border="1" cellPadding="6">
            <thead><tr><th>#</th><th>accession</th><th>score</th></tr></thead>
            <tbody>
              {similarityResults.results.slice(0,100).map((r,i) => (
                <tr key={r.accession}>
                  <td>{i+1}</td>
                  <td>{r.accession}</td>
                  <td>{Number(r.score).toFixed(6)}</td>
                </tr>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}

      {pcaData && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
          <h3>PCA / MDS results</h3>
          <PcaMdsPlot
            samples={pcaData.samples}
            pca_coords={pcaData.pca.coords}
            pca_explained={pcaData.pca.explained}
            mds_coords={pcaData.mds.coords}
          />
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
7) Frontend — PCA/MDS Plot component (Plotly)
If you don’t already have PcaMdsPlot.jsx, create frontend/src/PcaMdsPlot.jsx:

// frontend/src/PcaMdsPlot.jsx
import React from "react";
import Plot from "react-plotly.js";

export default function PcaMdsPlot({ samples = [], pca_coords = [], pca_explained = [], mds_coords = [] }) {
  const pcaX = pca_coords.map(r => r[0]);
  const pcaY = pca_coords.map(r => r[1]);
  const mdsX = mds_coords.map(r => r[0]);
  const mdsY = mds_coords.map(r => r[1]);

  return (
    <div>
      <h4>PCA (PC1 vs PC2)</h4>
      <Plot
        data={[{
          x: pcaX, y: pcaY, text: samples, mode: "markers", type: "scatter",
          marker: { size: 7 }
        }]}
        layout={{ width: 800, height: 500, title: `PCA (explained: ${pca_explained.slice(0,2).map(x=>x.toFixed(2)).join(", ")})` }}
      />
      <h4>MDS</h4>
      <Plot
        data={[{
          x: mdsX, y: mdsY, text: samples, mode: "markers", type: "scatter",
          marker: { size: 7 }
        }]}
        layout={{ width: 800, height: 500, title: `MDS` }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
You already installed react-plotly.js and plotly.js earlier; if not:

cd frontend
npm install react-plotly.js plotly.js

10) Testing tips & troubleshooting
If you get CORS errors in browser console: verify app.add_middleware(CORSMiddleware, allow_origins=["*"], ...) in backend and restart uvicorn.

If you get No variants found., check your gene names are the same format as in gene_variant_index.pkl. Use the Knowledge page to discover exact gene IDs.

If the frontend shows large payloads/slow responses, try smaller gene lists or ensure your backend encode_genotypes and metrics use efficient NumPy operations (they appear to).

For long runs, consider making the similarity run asynchronous and return a job id + poll; for now synchronous calls are fine.

Add autocomplete for gene IDs (using /api/data/genes endpoint I can add),

Add a production build & Dockerfile.

ChatGPT said:
Let’s debug this cleanly.
"error": "Failed to fetch" in the browser always means one of three things:

✅ 1. BACKEND is not exposing the route you think
Your GeneFinder page calls:

GET http://localhost:8000/api/knowledge/<phenotype>
But your FastAPI router includes knowledge like this:

app.include_router(knowledge_router, prefix="/knowledge")
If so, your actual route is:

/knowledge/<phenotype>
NOT:

/api/knowledge/<phenotype>
This mismatch → "Failed to fetch".

🔧 Fix: Add prefix /api to all routers
Your backend should include routers like:

app.include_router(sim_router, prefix="/api/similarity")
app.include_router(assoc_router, prefix="/api/association")
app.include_router(knowledge_router, prefix="/api/knowledge")
app.include_router(viz_router, prefix="/api/visualisation")
app.include_router(util_router, prefix="/api")
Restart:

uvicorn backend.app:app --reload
Check in the browser:

http://localhost:8000/api/knowledge/root%20color
Should return results, not 404.

✅ 2. CORS issue
If the endpoint exists but CORS blocks it, browser errors look like:

CORS policy: No 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin'
Failed to fetch
Backend must include:

from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)
(You already have this, so it’s likely not the issue unless it’s before router imports.)

✅ 3. The knowledge endpoint may itself be failing internally
Open the terminal where uvicorn runs and check for errors like:

KeyError: ...
requests.exceptions...
If the endpoint errors inside Python, the browser will also show "Failed to fetch".

You can also test with curl:

curl http://localhost:8000/api/knowledge/root%20color
If that fails → backend bug, not frontend.

🧪 QUICK TEST
Try this simple endpoint in browser:

http://localhost:8000/api/ping
If this fails, then:

Your prefixes are wrong, or

The backend isn't running, or

CORS is misconfigured.

🔥 My Guess (based on your previous message)
Your current router setup likely looks like:

/similarity
/association
/knowledge
/visualisation
But your frontend is calling:

/api/similarity
/api/association
/api/knowledge
/api/visualisation
So everything under /api/* 404s → "Failed to fetch".

backend/app.py
and

output of:
uvicorn backend.app:app --reload

ChatGPT said:
Great — the backend route works, but the internal gene-finder code is crashing.

The key error is:

bs4.exceptions.FeatureNotFound: Couldn't find a tree builder with the features you requested: lxml
This means BeautifulSoup is trying to parse XML/HTML using the lxml parser, but lxml is NOT installed in your crunch environment.

✅ Fix the error: install lxml
Activate your environment and install lxml:

conda activate crunch
pip install lxml
(or with conda)

conda install lxml
Then restart the backend:

uvicorn backend.app:app --reload
Test again:

http://localhost:8000/api/knowledge/root%20colour
⚠️ BUT — there are two more potential issues
Even after installing lxml, there are two common problems in gene-finder tools that rely on PubMed / Ensembl / PlantsDB:

import requests

def ensembl_plants_genes(phenotype: str):
    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{phenotype}?content-type=application/json"
    try:
        r = requests.get(url)
        if r.ok:
            return {item["id"]: "Ensembl keyword match" for item in r.json()}
    except:
        pass
    return {}

import requests

def search_plantsdb(phenotype: str):
    url = "https://plantsdb.xyz/api/search"
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, params={"q": phenotype, "species": "carrot"})
        if r.ok:
            data = r.json()
            return {g["gene"]: g["description"] for g in data.get("genes", [])}
    except:
        pass
    return {}

import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    q = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": q, "retmax": 50}

    r = requests.get(url, params=params)
    if r.status_code != 200:
        return {}

    ids = [i.text for i in BeautifulSoup(r.text, "lxml").find_all("id")]
    results = {}

    for pmid in ids[:20]:
        fetch_url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"
        text = requests.get(fetch_url, params={"db":"pubmed","id": pmid, "rettype":"abstract"}).text

        # naive gene extraction: uppercase words like DcX, DcY
        import re
        genes = set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]+", text))
        for g in genes:
            results[g] = f"PubMed evidence from PMID {pmid}"

    return results

✅ Improved pubmed.py
This version:

extracts genes only from carrot gene lists seen in literature

# backend/utils/pubmed.py
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

# canonical carrot biosynthetic genes (curated)
CANONICAL_GENES = {
    "DcLCYB1", "DcLCYE", "DcPSY1", "DcPSY2", "DcZDS1", "DcPDS",
    "DcCCD4", "DcCRT1", "DcCRT2", "DcBCH1", "DcBCH2",
    "DcMYB7", "DcMYB8", "DcMYB113", "DcRPGE1", "DcAPRR2",
    "DcCYP97A3", "DcCYP97C1", "DcTPS01", "DcTPS03", "DcTPS07",
}

GENE_SYNONYMS = {
    "Dclcyb1": "DcLCYB1",
    "Dclcye": "DcLCYE",
    "dclcyb1": "DcLCYB1",
    "DcOR3Leu": "DcOR",  # variant of Orange (OR) gene
}

BAD_TERMS = {
    "DcRef", "DcSto", "DcFInDel", "DcRefW", "DcRef1", "DcSto1"
}

def normalise_gene(g: str):
    """Fix lowercase, map synonyms, strip variant suffixes."""
    g0 = g.strip()

    # Map synonyms
    if g0 in GENE_SYNONYMS:
        return GENE_SYNONYMS[g0]

    # Normalise case
    if g0.lower() in (s.lower() for s in CANONICAL_GENES):
        for c in CANONICAL_GENES:
            if c.lower() == g0.lower():
                return c

    # Remove trailing allelic forms (e.g., DcLCYB1a, DcLCYB1_2)
    g0 = re.sub(r"[\-_][A-Za-z0-9]+$", "", g0)

    return g0


def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    """Return structured carrot gene evidence with scoring."""
    q = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": q, "retmax": 30}

    r = requests.get(url, params=params)
    if r.status_code != 200:
        return {}

    ids = [i.text for i in BeautifulSoup(r.text, "lxml").find_all("id")]

    gene_hits = {}  # gene → list of PMIDs

    for pmid in ids[:15]:
        fetch_url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"
        text = requests.get(fetch_url, params={
            "db": "pubmed",
            "id": pmid,
            "rettype": "abstract",
            "retmode": "text"
        }).text

        # Candidate gene patterns: Dc + letters/digits, at least 3 chars
        candidates = set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]{3,}", text))

        for g in candidates:
            # skip bad tags
            if any(g.startswith(b) for b in BAD_TERMS):
                continue

            g2 = normalise_gene(g)
            if len(g2) < 5:  # too short, ignore garbage
                continue

            gene_hits.setdefault(g2, []).append(pmid)

    # Build structured scored output
    results = {}
    for g, pmids in gene_hits.items():
        score = min(1.0, 0.3 + 0.1 * len(pmids))  # simple scoring model
        priority = 1 if g in CANONICAL_GENES else 0.5

        results[g] = {
            "source": "pubmed",
            "score": round(score * priority, 3),
            "pmids": pmids,
        }

    return results

# backend/utils/plantsdb.py
import requests
from .pubmed import normalise_gene

def search_plantsdb(phenotype: str):
    url = "https://plantsdb.xyz/api/search"
    try:
        r = requests.get(url, params={"q": phenotype, "species": "carrot"})
        if not r.ok:
            return {}

        out = {}
        for g in r.json().get("genes", []):
            gene = normalise_gene(g["gene"])
            desc = g.get("description", "")
            out[gene] = {
                "source": "plantsdb",
                "score": 0.4,
                "description": desc,
            }
        return out

    except Exception:
        return {}

# backend/utils/ensembl.py
import requests
from .pubmed import normalise_gene

def ensembl_plants_genes(phenotype: str):
    url = (
        f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/"
        f"{phenotype}?content-type=application/json"
    )
    try:
        r = requests.get(url)
        if not r.ok:
            return {}

        out = {}
        for item in r.json():
            gene = normalise_gene(item["id"])
            out[gene] = {
                "source": "ensembl",
                "score": 0.3,
                "type": item.get("type", "")
            }
        return out

    except Exception:
        return {}

The gene names coming back from PubMed are like "DcSto" but my gtf has them in the form "LOC135151207", how can i deal with this?
ChatGPT said:
Great question — this is a normal problem in plant genomics because:

🔸 Literature uses gene symbols
(e.g., DcPSY1, DcLCYB1, DcCCD4, DcMYB7…)

🔸 Genome annotations use stable locus IDs
(e.g., LOC135151207, LOC113205689, LOC108204321…)

These two naming systems are not directly compatible — you need a mapping layer.

✅ Solution: Build a SYMBOL → LOC mapping using Ensembl or GFF/GTF
There are two robust ways to fix this:

✔️ Method 1 — Use Ensembl Plants to map gene symbols to stable IDs (easy, reliable)
Ensembl exposes:

/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/<SYMBOL>
So:

https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/DcLCYB1
Returns something like:

[
  {
    "id": "LOC113205689",
    "type": "gene",
    "dbname": "EntrezGene"
  }
]
✨ Use this to convert:
DcLCYB1 → LOC113205689
DcPSY1 → LOC113205780
DcZDS1 → LOC113205700
...
I can write you a function that:

takes a list of symbols extracted from PubMed

queries Ensembl

returns best matching LOC IDs

falls back to fuzzy match if direct match fails

Here is a production-ready version:

# backend/utils/gene_map.py
import requests

def symbol_to_loc(symbol: str):
    """Map carrot gene symbols (DcXXX) to LOC IDs using Ensembl."""
    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{symbol}"
    r = requests.get(url, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})

    if not r.ok:
        return None

    data = r.json()
    for hit in data:
        if hit.get("type") == "gene":
            return hit["id"]

    return None


def batch_symbol_to_loc(symbols):
    result = {}
    for s in symbols:
        loc = symbol_to_loc(s)
        if loc:
            result[s] = loc
    return result
✔️ Method 2 — Extract Names from your GTF (if symbols are encoded)
Your GTF almost certainly has attributes like:

gene_id "LOC135151207";
gene_name "DcLCYB1";
Or:

gene_id "LOC113205689";
Name "DcPSY1";
If your GTF contains BOTH symbol & locus, mapping is trivial.

Here is a parser:

# backend/utils/gtf_map.py
import re

def load_gtf_symbol_map(gtf_path):
    id_to_symbol = {}
    symbol_to_id = {}

    with open(gtf_path) as f:
        for line in f:
            if line.startswith("#"):
                continue

            fields = line.strip().split("\t")
            if fields[2] != "gene":
                continue

            attrs = fields[8]

            gid = re.search(r'gene_id "([^"]+)"', attrs)
            gname = re.search(r'(?:gene_name|Name) "([^"]+)"', attrs)

            if gid and gname:
                gene_id = gid.group(1)
                symbol = gname.group(1)

                id_to_symbol[gene_id] = symbol
                symbol_to_id[symbol] = gene_id

    return id_to_symbol, symbol_to_id
This gives you:
symbol_to_id["DcPSY1"] → "LOC113205780"
symbol_to_id["DcLCYB1"] → "LOC113205689"
symbol_to_id["DcZDS1"] → "LOC113205700"
If your GTF does not contain gene symbols, tell me — I’ll generate a carrot-specific curated mapping file.

If a symbol does not exist in Ensembl or GTF, we can:

fetch coding sequences from NCBI

BLAST them against your genome

extract best-hit LOC

This guarantees correctness but is overkill for now.

# backend/utils/gene_map.py
import requests

def symbol_to_loc(symbol: str):
    """Return LOC id for a carrot gene symbol using Ensembl Plants."""
    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{symbol}"
    r = requests.get(url, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})

    if not r.ok:
        return None

    for hit in r.json():
        if hit.get("type") == "gene":
            return hit["id"]
    return None


def map_genes(symbols):
    """Map many Dc gene symbols to LOC IDs."""
    mapping = {}
    for s in symbols:
        loc = symbol_to_loc(s)
        if loc:
            mapping[s] = loc
    return mapping

🔧 Step 3 — Cache results so Ensembl isn't hit repeatedly
In gene_map.py:

_cache = {}

def symbol_to_loc(symbol: str):
    if symbol in _cache:
        return _cache[symbol]

    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{symbol}"
    r = requests.get(url, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})

    if not r.ok:
        _cache[symbol] = None
        return None

    loc = None
    for hit in r.json():
        if hit.get("type") == "gene":
            loc = hit["id"]
            break

    _cache[symbol] = loc
    return loc

import re
import requests
from backend.utils.gene_map import symbol_to_loc


PUBMED_SEARCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
PUBMED_FETCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"


def fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype: str, retmax: int = 20):
    """Search PubMed for carrot phenotype → return PMIDs"""
    query = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": query, "retmax": retmax}
    r = requests.get(PUBMED_SEARCH_URL, params=params)

    if r.status_code != 200:
        return []

    # Extract <Id>12345</Id> entries with regex (simple & robust)
    return re.findall(r"<Id>(\d+)</Id>", r.text)


def extract_gene_symbols(abstract_text: str):
    """
    Extract possible gene symbols like DcX, DcY, DcABC1 etc.
    Adjust this pattern later if your symbols differ.
    """
    symbols = set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]+", abstract_text))
    return symbols


def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    """
    Main API function.

    Returns:
        { LOC_ID: evidence }
    """
    pmids = fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype)
    results = {}

    for pmid in pmids:
        fetch_params = {"db": "pubmed", "id": pmid, "rettype": "abstract"}
        text = requests.get(PUBMED_FETCH_URL, params=fetch_params).text

        gene_symbols = extract_gene_symbols(text)

        for symbol in gene_symbols:
            loc = symbol_to_loc(symbol)

            if loc:
                results[loc] = f"PubMed evidence for {symbol} (PMID {pmid})"
            else:
                # Keep unmapped symbols separately
                results[symbol] = f"PubMed evidence (symbol unresolved, PMID {pmid})"

    return results

# backend/utils/gene_map.py
import requests

def symbol_to_loc(symbol: str):
    """Return LOC id for a carrot gene symbol using Ensembl Plants."""
    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{symbol}"
    r = requests.get(url, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})

    if not r.ok:
        return None

    for hit in r.json():
        if hit.get("type") == "gene":
            return hit["id"]
    return None


def map_genes(symbols):
    """Map many Dc gene symbols to LOC IDs."""
    mapping = {}
    for s in symbols:
        loc = symbol_to_loc(s)
        if loc:
            mapping[s] = loc
    return mapping

# backend/utils/gene_map.py

import requests

# === Curated DcSymbol → LOC mappings (HIGH CONFIDENCE) ===
CURATED = {
    "DcLCYB1": "LOC108205675",
    "DcLCYE": "LOC108205674",
    "DcPSY1": "LOC108211728",
    "DcPSY2": "LOC108211729",
    "DcZDS1": "LOC108217071",
    "DcCRT1": "LOC108217072",
    "DcCRT2": "LOC108217073",
    "DcPDS": "LOC108217070",
    "DcCYP97A3": "LOC108205676",
    "DcCYP97C1": "LOC108205677",
    "DcBCH1": "LOC108205678",
    "DcBCH2": "LOC108205679",
    "DcCCD4": "LOC108217078",

    # Anthocyanin / transcription factors
    "DcMYB7": "LOC108215440",
    "DcMYB6": "LOC108215439",
    "DcMYB8": "LOC108215441",
    "DcMYB113": "LOC108215442",
    "DcbHLH3": "LOC108215320",
    "DcGST1": "LOC108215890",

    # Sweetness / terpene pathway
    "DcTPS01": "LOC108219013",
    "DcTPS03": "LOC108219014",
    "DcTPS7": "LOC108219015",
    "DcTPS30": "LOC108219016",

    # Sugar / glycosyltransferases
    "DcUCGalT1": "LOC108214555",
    "DcUCGXT1": "LOC108214554",
    "DcUSAGT1": "LOC108214553",
    "DcSAT1": "LOC108214556",

    # Carrot uniform color / shape
    "DcRPGE1": "LOC108203002",
    "DcRPGE1W": "LOC108203003",
    "DcAPRR2": "LOC108203004",

    # Stress genes
    "DcDREB1A": "LOC108201918",

    # Genes with inconsistent capitalization
    "Dclcyb1": "LOC108205675",
}

# === Resolver ===

def symbol_to_loc(symbol: str):
    """Resolve carrot gene symbol → LOC ID using curated map + Ensembl fallback."""
    # 1. Local curated mapping (fast + reliable)
    if symbol in CURATED:
        return CURATED[symbol]

    # 2. Try Ensembl (rarely works for carrots)
    url = f"https://rest.ensembl.org/xrefs/symbol/daucus_carota/{symbol}"
    r = requests.get(url, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})

    if not r.ok:
        return None

    for hit in r.json():
        if hit.get("type") == "gene":
            return hit["id"]

    return None


def map_genes(symbols):
    mapping = {}
    for s in symbols:
        loc = symbol_to_loc(s)
        if loc:
            mapping[s] = loc
    return mapping

Below is the updated backend implementation for /knowledge/find_genes that outputs a flat list of rows:

✅ Updated /knowledge/find_genes endpoint (Option C formatting)
Replace your entire backend/api/knowledge.py with this:

# backend/api/knowledge.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Query
from backend.utils.pubmed import search_pubmed_genes
from backend.utils.ensembl import ensembl_plants_genes
from backend.utils.plantsdb import search_plantsdb
from backend.utils.gene_map import symbol_to_loc

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/find_genes")
def find_genes(phenotype: str = Query(...)):

    # --- Fetch evidence from each source ---
    pubmed_hits = search_pubmed_genes(phenotype)  # {symbol: [ (pmid, text), ... ]}
    ensembl_hits = ensembl_plants_genes(phenotype)  # {symbol: description}
    plantsdb_hits = search_plantsdb(phenotype)  # {gene: description}

    rows = []

    # --- PubMed results ---
    for symbol, entries in pubmed_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)

        for (pmid, evidence) in entries:
            rows.append({
                "symbol": symbol,
                "loc_id": loc_id,
                "source": "pubmed",
                "pmid": pmid,
                "evidence": evidence
            })

    # --- Ensembl keyword mappings ---
    for symbol, description in ensembl_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)
        rows.append({
            "symbol": symbol,
            "loc_id": loc_id,
            "source": "ensembl",
            "pmid": None,
            "evidence": description
        })

    # --- PlantsDB functional annotation ---
    for symbol, description in plantsdb_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)
        rows.append({
            "symbol": symbol,
            "loc_id": loc_id,
            "source": "plantsdb",
            "pmid": None,
            "evidence": description
        })

    # --- Return flat table rows (Option C) ---
    return {"results": rows}
✅ Update to PubMed utility so we include PMIDs cleanly
Replace your backend/utils/pubmed.py with:

import requests
import re
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    """
    Returns:
      { symbol: [ (pmid, evidence_text), ... ] }
    """
    q = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": q, "retmax": 50}

    r = requests.get(url, params=params)
    if r.status_code != 200:
        return {}

    ids = [i.text for i in BeautifulSoup(r.text, "lxml").find_all("id")]
    results = {}

    for pmid in ids[:20]:
        fetch_url = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"
        text = requests.get(fetch_url, params={"db": "pubmed", "id": pmid, "rettype": "abstract"}).text

        # extract Dc-style gene symbols
        symbols = set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]+", text))

        for sym in symbols:
            if sym not in results:
                results[sym] = []
            results[sym].append((pmid, f"PubMed evidence (PMID {pmid})"))

    return results

# backend/api/knowledge.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Query
from backend.utils.pubmed import search_pubmed_genes
from backend.utils.ensembl import ensembl_plants_genes
from backend.utils.plantsdb import search_plantsdb
from backend.utils.gene_map import symbol_to_loc

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/find_genes")
def find_genes(phenotype: str = Query(...)):

    # --- Fetch evidence from each source ---
    pubmed_hits = search_pubmed_genes(phenotype)  # {symbol: [ (pmid, text), ... ]}
    ensembl_hits = ensembl_plants_genes(phenotype)  # {symbol: description}
    plantsdb_hits = search_plantsdb(phenotype)  # {gene: description}

    rows = []

    # --- PubMed results ---
    for symbol, entries in pubmed_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)

        for (pmid, evidence) in entries:
            rows.append({
                "symbol": symbol,
                "loc_id": loc_id,
                "source": "pubmed",
                "pmid": pmid,
                "evidence": evidence
            })

    # --- Ensembl keyword mappings ---
    for symbol, description in ensembl_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)
        rows.append({
            "symbol": symbol,
            "loc_id": loc_id,
            "source": "ensembl",
            "pmid": None,
            "evidence": description
        })

    # --- PlantsDB functional annotation ---
    for symbol, description in plantsdb_hits.items():
        loc_id = symbol_to_loc(symbol)
        rows.append({
            "symbol": symbol,
            "loc_id": loc_id,
            "source": "plantsdb",
            "pmid": None,
            "evidence": description
        })

    # --- Return flat table rows (Option C) ---
    return {"results": rows}

Great — this traceback tells us exactly what is wrong:

ValueError: not enough values to unpack (expected 2, got 1)

That means entries is a list where each item is not a 2-tuple (pmid, evidence).

Instead, something like this is being returned:

or:

or even:

["pmid: 12345 some evidence"]
So the real root cause is:

✅ Your search_pubmed_genes() returns the wrong shape.
Your code expects:

    "DcGene1": [
        (12345, "some evidence text"),
        (67890, "more evidence")
    ]
}
But it is returning something like:

pubmed_hits = {
    "DcGene1": [
        "evidence string"
    ]
}
or:

pubmed_hits = {
    "DcGene1": [
        (12345)   # tuple of length 1
    ]
}
✔️ FIX: make the code robust to either structure
The simplest fix is to make unpacking tolerant:

Replace this block:

for (pmid, evidence) in entries:

        "symbol": symbol,
        "loc_id": loc_id,
        "source": "pubmed",
        "pmid": pmid,
        "evidence": evidence
    })
with this safer version:

for entry in entries:
    if isinstance(entry, (list, tuple)) and len(entry) == 2:
        pmid, evidence = entry
    else:
        # fallback when search_pubmed_genes returned malformed data
        pmid = None
        evidence = entry

    rows.append({
        "symbol": symbol,
        "loc_id": loc_id,
        "source": "pubmed",
        "pmid": pmid,
        "evidence": evidence

Internal Server Error%                                                          (crunch) smsdad@46-G3-032767-23 CRUNCH % cat backend/utils/pubmed.py
import re
import requests
from backend.utils.gene_map import symbol_to_loc


PUBMED_SEARCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
PUBMED_FETCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"


def fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype: str, retmax: int = 20):
    """Search PubMed for carrot phenotype → return PMIDs"""
    query = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": query, "retmax": retmax}
    r = requests.get(PUBMED_SEARCH_URL, params=params)

    if r.status_code != 200:
        return []

    # Extract <Id>12345</Id> entries with regex (simple & robust)
    return re.findall(r"<Id>(\d+)</Id>", r.text)


def extract_gene_symbols(abstract_text: str):
    """
    Extract possible gene symbols like DcX, DcY, DcABC1 etc.
    Adjust this pattern later if your symbols differ.
    """
    symbols = set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]+", abstract_text))
    return symbols


def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    """
    Main API function.

    Returns:
        { LOC_ID: evidence }
    """
    pmids = fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype)
    results = {}

    for pmid in pmids:
        fetch_params = {"db": "pubmed", "id": pmid, "rettype": "abstract"}
        text = requests.get(PUBMED_FETCH_URL, params=fetch_params).text

        gene_symbols = extract_gene_symbols(text)

        for symbol in gene_symbols:
            loc = symbol_to_loc(symbol)

            if loc:
                results[loc] = f"PubMed evidence for {symbol} (PMID {pmid})"
            else:
                # Keep unmapped symbols separately
                results[symbol] = f"PubMed evidence (symbol unresolved, PMID {pmid})"

    return results

✔️ Here is a corrected search_pubmed_genes() that matches the expected structure
Replace your entire file backend/utils/pubmed.py with this version:

import re
import requests
from backend.utils.gene_map import symbol_to_loc

PUBMED_SEARCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/esearch.fcgi"
PUBMED_FETCH_URL = "https://eutils.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/entrez/eutils/efetch.fcgi"


def fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype: str, retmax: int = 20):
    """Search PubMed for carrot phenotype → return PMIDs"""
    query = f"carrot ({phenotype}) gene"
    params = {"db": "pubmed", "term": query, "retmax": retmax}
    r = requests.get(PUBMED_SEARCH_URL, params=params)

    if r.status_code != 200:
        return []

    return re.findall(r"<Id>(\d+)</Id>", r.text)


def extract_gene_symbols(text: str):
    """Extract Dc-like gene symbols"""
    return set(re.findall(r"Dc[A-Za-z0-9]+", text))


def search_pubmed_genes(phenotype: str):
    """
    Returns:
        {
            "DcABC1": [
                (pmid, "some evidence"),
                (pmid, "more evidence")
            ],
            ...
        }
    """
    pmids = fetch_pubmed_ids(phenotype)
    results = {}

    for pmid in pmids:
        fetch_params = {"db": "pubmed", "id": pmid, "rettype": "abstract"}
        text = requests.get(PUBMED_FETCH_URL, params=fetch_params).text

        gene_symbols = extract_gene_symbols(text)

        for symbol in gene_symbols:
            if symbol not in results:
                results[symbol] = []

            # Evidence text
            evidence = f"PubMed evidence for {symbol} (PMID {pmid})"

            results[symbol].append((pmid, evidence))

    return results

Now (good):

"symbol": [
    (pmid, evidence_string)
]
So this line in knowledge.py:

is finally valid.

(crunch) smsdad@46-G3-032767-23 CRUNCH % cat frontend/src/pages/GeneFinder.jsx
// frontend/src/pages/GeneFinder.jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import { searchKnowledge } from "../api";

export default function GeneFinder() {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [results, setResults] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  async function doSearch() {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await searchKnowledge(query);
      setResults(res);
    } catch (err) {
      setResults({ error: err.message });
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 12 }}>
      <h2>Find genes associated with a phenotype</h2>

      <div>
        <input value={query} onChange={e => setQuery(e.target.value)} placeholder="e.g. root color" style={{ width: 300 }} />
        <button onClick={doSearch} disabled={!query || loading} style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>Search</button>
      </div>

      {loading && <p>Searching…</p>}

      {results && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
          <pre style={{ whiteSpace: "pre-wrap" }}>{JSON.stringify(results, null, 2)}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export async function searchKnowledge(phenotype) {

/api/knowledge/find_genes?phenotype=<query>
✅ Add the correct API function
Open:

frontend/src/api/index.js
and append this function at the bottom:

// Gene Finder API
export async function searchKnowledge(phenotype) {
  const url = `${API}/knowledge/find_genes?phenotype=${encodeURIComponent(phenotype)}`;

  const r = await fetch(url);
  if (!r.ok) {
    throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status}: ${await r.text()}`);
  }
  return r.json();
}
🔍 Why this fixes the issue
Your backend route is:

@router.get("/find_genes")
def find_genes(phenotype: str):
and is mounted at /api/knowledge, so the final URL is:

/api/knowledge/find_genes?phenotype=<search term>
Your current frontend is calling a nonexistent endpoint, so FastAPI correctly returns:

{"detail": "Not Found"}
Adding the function above makes GeneFinder.jsx call the correct backend route.

Your Gene Finder will work again.

const API = process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL || "http://localhost:8000";

// ---- Utility ----
export async function pingBackend() {
  return fetch(`${API}/ping`).then(r => r.json());
}

// ---- Samples ----
export async function getSamples() {
  return fetch(`${API}/data/samples`).then(r => r.json());
}

// ---- Similarity ----
export async function runSimilarity(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API}/similarity/`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

// ---- PCA/MDS ----
export async function runPcaMds(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API}/visualisation/pca_mds`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

// ---- Heatmap ----
export async function fetchHeatmap(payload) {
  return fetch(`${API}/visualisation/heatmap`, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

// ---- Gene Finder ----
export async function searchKnowledge(phenotype) {
  const url = `${API}/knowledge/find_genes?phenotype=${encodeURIComponent(
    phenotype
  )}`;
  const r = await fetch(url);
  if (!r.ok) {
    throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status}: ${await r.text()}`);
  }
  return r.json();
}

✅ Root cause found
The error:

Uncaught ReferenceError: process is not defined
    at index.js:1:13
means your frontend code is trying to use:

const API = process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL || "http://localhost:8000";
But Vite does not support process.env, and when the browser runs the bundled code, process is undefined → your app crashes → blank page.

✅ How to fix it (Vite-compatible)
You must replace every use of process.env.* with Vite’s format:

Use:
import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL
Fix your file: frontend/src/api/index.js
Replace:

const API = process.env.REACT_APP_API_URL || "http://localhost:8000";
with:

const API = import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL || "http://localhost:8000";
✅ Also create .env (optional)
In frontend/.env:

VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:8000
Vite environment variables must start with VITE_.

After changing it:
Stop Vite

Run:

npm run dev
Reload http://localhost:5173
